<pr_description>
No VM metrics with Centos/RHEL for Openstack
### Kepler Version

0.10.0 or later (Current/Supported)

### Bug Description

On Openstack for exemple, the virtual machine hypervisor is provided by install qem-kvm:
```
qemu-kvm-core-17:8.2.0-11.el9_4.14.x86_64 : qemu-kvm core components                                                           
Repo        : rhosp-rhel-9.4-appstream
Matched from:                      
Filename    : /usr/libexec/qemu-kvm
```
Then the usage is like: 
`/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm -name guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on -S -object {"qom-type":"secret","id":"masterKey0","format":"raw","file":"/var/lib/libvirt/qemu/domain-25-instance-0000008b/master-key.aes"} -machine pc-q35-rhel9.4.0,usb=off,dump-guest-core=off,hpet=off,acpi=on -accel kvm -cpu Broadwell-IBRS [...] `

So of course, because Kepler is only looking for: 
https://github.com/sustainable-computing-io/kepler/blob/0339f536e97ec74a3813fa784bd5f4d489d75891/internal/resource/vm.go#L15

then it can't work...

### Steps to Reproduce

RHEL/CentOS: yum install qemu-kvm-core

### Expected Behavior

kepler_vm_* metrics are present with the right information of the VM. 

### Environment

Any Centos / RHEL

### Logs and Error Messages

```shell

```

### Additional Context

_No response_

     1	// SPDX-FileCopyrightText: 2025 The Kepler Authors
     2	// SPDX-License-Identifier: Apache-2.0
     3	
     4	package resource
     5	
     6	import (
     7	        "fmt"
     8	        "path/filepath"
     9	        "regexp"
    10	        "strings"
    11	)
    12	
    13	var (
    14	        // QEMU/KVM patterns
    15	        qemuPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`bin/qemu-system-\w+`)
    16	
    17	        // TODO: add patterns for virtual box,  VMware, Xen
    18	
    19	        // VM process name patterns
    20	        vmProcessPatterns = map[*regexp.Regexp]Hypervisor{
    21	                qemuPattern: KVMHypervisor,
    22	        }
    23	)
    24	
    25	// vmInfoFromProc detects if a process is a VM process and extracts VM info
    26	func vmInfoFromProc(proc procInfo) (*VirtualMachine, error) {
    27	        // Check command line for VM processes
    28	        cmdline, err := proc.CmdLine()
    29	        if err != nil {
    30	                return nil, fmt.Errorf("failed to get process cmdline: %w", err)
    31	        }
    32	
    33	        if len(cmdline) == 0 {
    34	                return nil, nil
    35	        }
    36	
    37	        hypervisor, vmID := vmInfoFromCmdLine(cmdline)
    38	        if hypervisor == UnknownHypervisor {
    39	                return nil, nil
    40	        }
    41	
    42	        vm := &VirtualMachine{
    43	                ID:         vmID,
    44	                Hypervisor: hypervisor,
    45	        }
    46	
    47	        // Try to get VM name from command line arguments
    48	        vm.Name = vmNameFromCmdLine(cmdline, hypervisor)
    49	
    50	        if vm.Name == "" {
    51	                vm.Name = fmt.Sprintf("%s-%s", hypervisor, vmID[:8])
    52	        }
    53	
    54	        return vm, nil
    55	}
    56	
    57	// vmInfoFromCmdLine extracts VM information from command line
    58	func vmInfoFromCmdLine(cmdline []string) (Hypervisor, string) {
    59	        if len(cmdline) == 0 {
    60	                return UnknownHypervisor, ""
    61	        }
    62	        exe := filepath.Base(cmdline[0])
    63	        fullCmd := strings.Join(cmdline, " ")
    64	
    65	        for pattern, hypervisor := range vmProcessPatterns {
    66	                if pattern.MatchString(exe) || pattern.MatchString(fullCmd) {
    67	                        vmID := extractVMID(cmdline, hypervisor)
    68	
    69	                        // If VM ID is still empty, make one up from the command line parameter hash
    70	                        // TODO: validate if this this is a good idea
    71	                        if vmID == "" {
    72	                                vmID = generateVMID(fullCmd)
    73	                        }
    74	                        return hypervisor, vmID
    75	                }
    76	        }
    77	
    78	        return UnknownHypervisor, ""
    79	}
    80	
    81	// extractVMID extracts VM ID from command line arguments based on hypervisor
    82	func extractVMID(cmdline []string, hypervisor Hypervisor) string {
    83	        switch hypervisor {
    84	        case KVMHypervisor:
    85	                return extractQemuMachineID(cmdline)
    86	        default:
    87	                return ""
    88	        }
    89	}
    90	
    91	// extractQemuMachineID extracts VM ID from QEMU/KVM command line arguments, if present
    92	// otherwise returns the VM name
    93	func extractQemuMachineID(cmdline []string) string {
    94	        for i, arg := range cmdline {
    95	                if arg == "-uuid" && i+1 < len(cmdline) {
    96	                        return cmdline[i+1]
    97	                }
    98	        }
    99	        return qemuVMNameFromCmdLine(cmdline)
   100	}
   101	
   102	// generateVMID generates a VM ID when one can't be extracted
   103	func generateVMID(fullCmd string) string {
   104	        hash := fmt.Sprintf("%x", []byte(fullCmd))
   105	        if len(hash) > 16 {
   106	                return hash[:16]
   107	        }
   108	        return hash
   109	}
   110	
   111	// vmNameFromCmdLine extracts VM name from command line arguments
   112	func vmNameFromCmdLine(cmdline []string, hypervisor Hypervisor) string {
   113	        switch hypervisor {
   114	        case KVMHypervisor:
   115	                return qemuVMNameFromCmdLine(cmdline)
   116	        default:
   117	                return ""
   118	        }
   119	}
   120	
   121	// qemuVMNameFromCmdLine extracts VM name from QEMU command line
   122	func qemuVMNameFromCmdLine(cmdline []string) string {
   123	        for i, arg := range cmdline {
   124	                if arg == "-name" && i+1 < len(cmdline) {
   125	                        value := cmdline[i+1]
   126	                        // QEMU -name can have format "guest=name,debug-threads=on"
   127	                        if strings.Contains(value, "guest=") {
   128	                                parts := strings.Split(value, ",")
   129	
   130	                                for _, part := range parts {
   131	                                        if strings.HasPrefix(part, "guest=") {
   132	                                                return strings.TrimPrefix(part, "guest=")
   133	                                        }
   134	                                }
   135	                        }
   136	                        return value
   137	                }
   138	
   139	                if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-name=") {
   140	                        return strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "-name=")
   141	                }
   142	        }
   143	        return ""
   144	}
   145

Now I understand the issue. The problem is that on CentOS/RHEL systems, QEMU/KVM is installed as `/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm` rather than the pattern `/bin/qemu-system-\w+` that Kepler is currently looking for. The regex pattern on line 15 of `/testbed/internal/resource/vm.go` only matches processes in the `bin` directory with the pattern `qemu-system-*`, but it doesn't match the CentOS/RHEL path `/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm`.

Let me create a test script to reproduce the issue first:

import (
	"fmt"
	"regexp"
)

func main() {
	// Current pattern from vm.go
	qemuPattern := regexp.MustCompile(`bin/qemu-system-\w+`)
	
	// Test cases
	testCases := []string{
		"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",  // Standard Linux path
		"/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",      // Alternative path
		"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",        // CentOS/RHEL path (this should match but doesn'"'"'t)
		"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm-core",   // Possible variation
		"/usr/bin/qemu-kvm",            // Another possible path
		"/bin/kvm",                     // Simple kvm binary
	}
	
	fmt.Println("Testing current pattern:")
	for _, test := range testCases {
		matches := qemuPattern.MatchString(test)
		fmt.Printf("%-30s matches: %v\n", test, matches)
	}
	
	// Test with full command lines
	fmt.Println("\nTesting with full command lines:")
	fullCommands := []string{
		"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm -name guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on -S -object",
		"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64 -name guest=vm1,debug-threads=on",
	}
	
	for _, cmd := range fullCommands {
		matches := qemuPattern.MatchString(cmd)
		fmt.Printf("%-60s matches: %v\n", cmd, matches)
	}
}'

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_vm_detection.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"github.com/sustainable-computing-io/kepler/internal/resource"
)

func main() {
	// Test cases representing different QEMU/KVM command lines
	testCases := []struct {
		name    string
		cmdline []string
	}{
		{
			name:    "Standard QEMU",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64", "-name", "guest=vm1,debug-threads=on", "-machine", "pc"},
		},
		{
			name:    "CentOS/RHEL QEMU-KVM",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm", "-name", "guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on", "-S", "-object"},
		},
		{
			name:    "Alternative QEMU-KVM",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu-kvm", "-name", "guest=test-vm,debug-threads=on"},
		},
	}

	for _, tc := range testCases {
		fmt.Printf("\nTest: %s\n", tc.name)
		fmt.Printf("Command line: %v\n", tc.cmdline)
		
		// This simulates what vmInfoFromCmdLine does
		extractedInfo(tc.cmdline)
	}
}

func extractedInfo(cmdline []string) {
	// Simulate the vmInfoFromCmdLine logic
	exe := cmdline[0]
	fullCmd := ""
	for _, arg := range cmdline {
		fullCmd += arg + " "
	}
	
	fmt.Printf("Executable: %s\n", exe)
	fmt.Printf("Detected as VM: %v\n", isVMBinary(exe) || isVMBinaryFullCmd(fullCmd))
}

// Simulate the current pattern matching
func isVMBinary(exe string) bool {
	// Current pattern from vm.go
	qemuPattern := `bin/qemu-system-\w+`
	return matchPattern(exe, qemuPattern)
}

func isVMBinaryFullCmd(fullCmd string) bool {
	qemuPattern := `bin/qemu-system-\w+`
	return matchPattern(fullCmd, qemuPattern)
}

func matchPattern(s, pattern string) bool {
	// Simple substring matching for demonstration
	return contains(s, "qemu-system-")
}

func contains(s, substr string) bool {
	for i := 0; i <= len(s)-len(substr); i++ {
		if s[i:i+len(substr)] == substr {
			return true
		}
	}
	return false
}'

// Simulate the current pattern matching
func isVMBinary(exe string) bool {
	// Current pattern from vm.go
	qemuPattern := `bin/qemu-system-\w+`
	return matchPattern(exe, qemuPattern)
}

func isVMBinaryFullCmd(fullCmd string) bool {
	qemuPattern := `bin/qemu-system-\w+`
	return matchPattern(fullCmd, qemuPattern)
}

func matchPattern(s, pattern string) bool {
	// Simple substring matching for demonstration
	return contains(s, "qemu-system-")
}

func contains(s, substr string) bool {
	for i := 0; i <= len(s)-len(substr); i++ {
		if s[i:i+len(substr)] == substr {
			return true
		}
	}
	return false
}' --new_str 'func extractedInfo(cmdline []string) {
	// Simulate the vmInfoFromCmdLine logic
	exe := cmdline[0]
	fullCmd := ""
	for _, arg := range cmdline {
		fullCmd += arg + " "
	}
	
	// Use actual regex patterns like in vm.go
	qemuPattern := regexp.MustCompile(`bin/qemu-system-\w+`)
	
	matchesExe := qemuPattern.MatchString(exe)
	matchesFull := qemuPattern.MatchString(fullCmd)
	
	fmt.Printf("Executable: %s\n", exe)
	fmt.Printf("Matches executable: %v\n", matchesExe)
	fmt.Printf("Matches full command: %v\n", matchesFull)
	fmt.Printf("Detected as VM: %v\n", matchesExe || matchesFull)

Now I understand the issue. The current regex pattern `bin/qemu-system-\w+` only matches paths containing "qemu-system-" but not "qemu-kvm" which is used in CentOS/RHEL. Let me examine the current pattern more closely and create a better solution

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_new_patterns.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"regexp"
)

func main() {
	// Test cases representing different QEMU/KVM command lines
	testCases := []struct {
		name    string
		cmdline []string
	}{
		{
			name:    "Standard QEMU",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64", "-name", "guest=vm1,debug-threads=on", "-machine", "pc"},
		},
		{
			name:    "CentOS/RHEL QEMU-KVM",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm", "-name", "guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on", "-S", "-object"},
		},
		{
			name:    "Alternative QEMU-KVM",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu-kvm", "-name", "guest=test-vm,debug-threads=on"},
		},
		{
			name:    "Simple QEMU",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu", "-name", "guest=vm1"},
		},
		{
			name:    "KVM only",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/kvm", "-name", "guest=vm1"},
		},
	}

	// Test different patterns
	patterns := []struct {
		name string
		regex string
	}{
		{"Current", `bin/qemu-system-\w+`},
		{"QEMU variants", `(qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm|qemu)`},
		{"Flexible QEMU/KVM", `(qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm|qemu|kvm)`},
		{"Flexible with paths", `(bin|libexec)/(qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm|qemu|kvm)`},
	}

	for _, pattern := range patterns {
		fmt.Printf("\n=== Testing pattern: %s (%s) ===\n", pattern.name, pattern.regex)
		re := regexp.MustCompile(pattern.regex)
		
		for _, tc := range testCases {
			exe := tc.cmdline[0]
			fullCmd := ""
			for _, arg := range tc.cmdline {
				fullCmd += arg + " "
			}
			
			matchesExe := re.MatchString(exe)
			matchesFull := re.MatchString(fullCmd)
			
			fmt.Printf("%-30s | exe: %-5v | full: %-5v | detected: %v\n", 
				tc.name, matchesExe, matchesFull, matchesExe || matchesFull)
		}
	}
}'

    58	func vmInfoFromCmdLine(cmdline []string) (Hypervisor, string) {
    59	        if len(cmdline) == 0 {
    60	                return UnknownHypervisor, ""
    61	        }
    62	        exe := filepath.Base(cmdline[0])
    63	        fullCmd := strings.Join(cmdline, " ")
    64	
    65	        for pattern, hypervisor := range vmProcessPatterns {
    66	                if pattern.MatchString(exe) || pattern.MatchString(fullCmd) {
    67	                        vmID := extractVMID(cmdline, hypervisor)
    68	
    69	                        // If VM ID is still empty, make one up from the command line parameter hash

    72	                                vmID = generateVMID(fullCmd)
    73	                        }

Perfect! Now I understand the issue completely. The code checks both the executable name (`exe`) and the full command line (`fullCmd`) against the regex pattern. On line 62, it uses `filepath.Base(cmdline[0])` which extracts just the filename, not the full path. This means we need a pattern that matches:

1. `qemu-system-x86_64` (from the executable name)
2. `/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64` (from the full command line)
3. `qemu-kvm` (from the executable name on CentOS/RHEL)
4. `/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm` (from the full command line on CentOS/RHEL)

I need to update the regex pattern to be more flexible. Let me create a test to confirm the current behavior first:

import (

	paths := []string{

		"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",

		"/usr/bin/qemu",
		"/usr/bin/kvm",
	}
	
	for _, path := range paths {
		base := filepath.Base(path)
		fmt.Printf("Path: %-30s | Base: %s\n", path, base)
	}
}'

Now I understand the issue better. Looking at the code flow:

1. In `vmInfoFromCmdLine`, the executable path is extracted using `filepath.Base(cmdline[0])`, which gives us just the binary name (e.g., "qemu-kvm" instead of "/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm")
2. The current pattern `bin/qemu-system-\w+` only matches paths containing "bin/qemu-system-" but doesn't match the base name "qemu-kvm"

The fix needs to match both the full path AND the base executable name. Let me implement the fix:

		qemuPattern: KVMHypervisor,
	}

	// QEMU/KVM patterns

	// VM process name patterns
	vmProcessPatterns = map[*regexp.Regexp]Hypervisor{
		qemuPattern: KVMHypervisor,

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_fixed_pattern.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"regexp"
)

func main() {
	// Test the new pattern
	qemuPattern := regexp.MustCompile(`(bin/qemu-system-\w+|qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm|qemu|kvm)`)
	
	// Test cases representing different QEMU/KVM command lines
	testCases := []struct {
		name    string
		cmdline []string
	}{
		{
			name:    "Standard QEMU",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64", "-name", "guest=vm1,debug-threads=on", "-machine", "pc"},
		},
		{
			name:    "CentOS/RHEL QEMU-KVM",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm", "-name", "guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on", "-S", "-object"},
		},
		{
			name:    "Alternative QEMU-KVM",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu-kvm", "-name", "guest=test-vm,debug-threads=on"},
		},
		{
			name:    "Simple QEMU",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu", "-name", "guest=vm1"},
		},
		{
			name:    "KVM only",
			cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/kvm", "-name", "guest=vm1"},
		},
	}

	for _, tc := range testCases {
		// Simulate vmInfoFromCmdLine logic
		exe := tc.cmdline[0]
		fullCmd := ""
		for _, arg := range tc.cmdline {
			fullCmd += arg + " "
		}
		
		matchesExe := qemuPattern.MatchString(exe)
		matchesFull := qemuPattern.MatchString(fullCmd)
		detected := matchesExe || matchesFull
		
		fmt.Printf("%-30s | exe: %-5v | full: %-5v | detected: %v\n", 
			tc.name, matchesExe, matchesFull, detected)
	}
}'

   235	func TestVMInfoFromProc(t *testing.T) {
   236	        type expect struct {
   237	                vm    *VirtualMachine
   238	                error bool
   239	        }
   240	
   241	        tests := []struct {
   242	                name         string
   243	                cmdline      []string
   244	                cmdlineError error
   245	                expected     expect
   246	        }{{
   247	                name: "QEMU VM with complete info",
   248	                cmdline: []string{
   249	                        "/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
   250	                        "-name", "guest=kepler-stuff_default,debug-threads=on",
   251	                        "-uuid", "df12672f-fedb-4f6f-9d51-0166868835fb",
   252	                },
   253	                expected: expect{
   254	                        vm: &VirtualMachine{
   255	                                ID:         "df12672f-fedb-4f6f-9d51-0166868835fb",
   256	                                Name:       "kepler-stuff_default",
   257	                                Hypervisor: KVMHypervisor,
   258	                        },
   259	                        error: false,
   260	                },
   261	        }, {
   262	                name: "QEMU VM without UUID",
   263	                cmdline: []string{
   264	                        "/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
   265	                        "-name", "guest=test-vm",
   266	                },
   267	                expected: expect{
   268	                        vm: &VirtualMachine{
   269	                                ID:         "test-vm",
   270	                                Name:       "test-vm",
   271	                                Hypervisor: KVMHypervisor,
   272	                        },
   273	                        error: false,
   274	                },
   275	        }, {
   276	                name: "QEMU VM without name (generates name)",
   277	                cmdline: []string{
   278	                        "/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
   279	                        "-uuid", "df12672f-fedb-4f6f-9d51-0166868835fb",
   280	                },
   281	                expected: expect{
   282	                        vm: &VirtualMachine{
   283	                                ID:         "df12672f-fedb-4f6f-9d51-0166868835fb",
   284	                                Name:       "kvm-df12672f",
   285	                                Hypervisor: KVMHypervisor,
   286	                        },
   287	                        error: false,
   288	                },
   289	        }, {
   290	                name: "Not a VM process",
   291	                cmdline: []string{
   292	                        "/usr/bin/firefox",
   293	                        "--profile", "/home/user/.mozilla/firefox",
   294	                },
   295	                expected: expect{nil, false},
   296	        }, {
   297	                name:         "Error reading cmdline",
   298	                cmdline:      nil,
   299	                cmdlineError: assert.AnError,
   300	                expected:     expect{nil, true},
   301	        }, {
   302	                name:     "Empty cmdline",
   303	                cmdline:  []string{},
   304	                expected: expect{nil, false},
   305	        }}
   306	
   307	        for _, tc := range tests {
   308	                t.Run(tc.name, func(t *testing.T) {
   309	                        mockProc := &MockProcInfo{}
   310	                        mockProc.On("CmdLine").Return(tc.cmdline, tc.cmdlineError)
   311	
   312	                        vm, err := vmInfoFromProc(mockProc)
   313	
   314	                        if tc.expected.error {
   315	                                assert.Error(t, err)
   316	                                return
   317	                        }
   318	
   319	                        assert.NoError(t, err)
   320	
   321	                        if tc.expected.vm == nil {
   322	                                assert.Nil(t, vm)
   323	                                return
   324	                        }
   325	
   326	                        require.NotNil(t, vm)
   327	                        assert.Equal(t, tc.expected.vm.ID, vm.ID)
   328	                        assert.Equal(t, tc.expected.vm.Name, vm.Name)
   329	                        assert.Equal(t, tc.expected.vm.Hypervisor, vm.Hypervisor)
   330	
   331	                        mockProc.AssertExpectations(t)
   332	                })
   333	        }
   334	}

   336	func TestVMClone(t *testing.T) {
   337	        t.Run("Full VM clone", func(t *testing.T) {
   338	                original := &VirtualMachine{
   339	                        ID:           "df12672f-fedb-4f6f-9d51-0166868835fb",
   340	                        Name:         "test-vm",
   341	                        Hypervisor:   KVMHypervisor,
   342	                        CPUTimeDelta: 123.45,
   343	                }
   344	
   345	                clone := original.Clone()
   346	
   347	                // Check that the clone has the same values
   348	                assert.Equal(t, original.ID, clone.ID)
   349	                assert.Equal(t, original.Name, clone.Name)
   350	                assert.Equal(t, original.Hypervisor, clone.Hypervisor)
   351	                assert.Equal(t, float64(0), clone.CPUTimeDelta) // CPUTime shouldn't be cloned
   352	        })
   353	
   354	        t.Run("Clone nil VM", func(t *testing.T) {
   355	                var nilVM *VirtualMachine
   356	                nilClone := nilVM.Clone()
   357	                assert.Nil(t, nilClone, "Cloning nil VM should return nil")
   358	        })
   359	}

str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_centos_pattern.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"path/filepath"
	"strings"
)

func main() {
	// Test the exact command from the PR description
	centosCommand := []string{
		"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
		"-name",
		"guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on",
		"-S",
		"-object",
		`{"qom-type":"secret","id":"masterKey0","format":"raw","file":"/var/lib/libvirt/qemu/domain-25-instance-0000008b/master-key.aes"}`,
		"-machine",
		"pc-q35-rhel9.4.0,usb=off,dump-guest-core=off,hpet=off,acpi=on",
		"-accel",
		"kvm",
		"-cpu",
		"Broadwell-IBRS",
	}

	// Simulate what vmInfoFromCmdLine does
	exe := filepath.Base(centosCommand[0])
	fullCmd := strings.Join(centosCommand, " ")
	
	fmt.Printf("Executable: %s\n", exe)
	fmt.Printf("Executable matches qemu-kvm: %v\n", strings.Contains(exe, "qemu-kvm"))
	fmt.Printf("Full command contains '"'"'qemu-kvm'"'"': %v\n", strings.Contains(fullCmd, "qemu-kvm"))
	fmt.Printf("Full command contains '"'"'-name guest='"'"': %v\n", strings.Contains(fullCmd, "-name guest="))
	
	// Test with our new pattern
	qemuPattern := `(bin/qemu-system-\w+|qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm|qemu|kvm)`
	
	fmt.Printf("\nPattern would match executable: %v\n", matchPattern(exe, qemuPattern))
	fmt.Printf("Pattern would match full command: %v\n", matchPattern(fullCmd, qemuPattern))
	
	// Test VM name extraction
	fmt.Printf("\nWould extract VM name: %v\n", extractVMName(centosCommand))
}

func matchPattern(s, pattern string) bool {
	// Simplified pattern matching for testing
	patterns := []string{"qemu-system-", "qemu-kvm", "qemu", "kvm"}
	for _, p := range patterns {
		if strings.Contains(s, p) {
			return true
		}
	}
	return false
}

func extractVMName(cmdline []string) string {
	for i, arg := range cmdline {
		if arg == "-name" && i+1 < len(cmdline) {
			value := cmdline[i+1]
			if strings.Contains(value, "guest=") {
				parts := strings.Split(value, ",")
				for _, part := range parts {
					if strings.HasPrefix(part, "guest=") {
						return strings.TrimPrefix(part, "guest=")
					}
				}
			}
			return value
		}
		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-name=") {
			return strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "-name=")
		}
	}
	return ""
}'

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"
	"path/filepath"
	"strings"

	"github.com/sustainable-computing-io/kepler/internal/resource"
)

func main() {
	// Test cases based on the PR description and common CentOS/RHEL scenarios
	testCases := []struct {
		name        string
		cmdline     []string
		expectedVM  bool
		expectedID  string
		expectedName string
	}{
		{
			name: "CentOS/RHEL OpenStack QEMU-KVM (from PR description)",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
				"-name", 
				"guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on",
				"-S",
				"-object",
				`{"qom-type":"secret","id":"masterKey0","format":"raw","file":"/var/lib/libvirt/qemu/domain-25-instance-0000008b/master-key.aes"}`,
				"-machine",
				"pc-q35-rhel9.4.0,usb=off,dump-guest-core=off,hpet=off,acpi=on",
				"-accel",
				"kvm",
				"-cpu",
				"Broadwell-IBRS",
			},
			expectedVM:  true,
			expectedID:  "instance-0000008b",
			expectedName: "instance-0000008b",
		},
		{
			name: "Standard QEMU system (original case)",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
				"-name",
				"guest=ubuntu-vm",
				"-uuid",
				"12345678-1234-5678-9abc-123456789abc",
			},
			expectedVM:  true,
			expectedID:  "12345678-1234-5678-9abc-123456789abc",
			expectedName: "ubuntu-vm",
		},
		{
			name: "Alternative QEMU-KVM path",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-kvm",
				"-name",
				"guest=centos-vm",
			},
			expectedVM:  true,
			expectedID:  "centos-vm",
			expectedName: "centos-vm",
		},
		{
			name: "Simple qemu binary",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu",
				"-name",
				"guest=simple-vm",
			},
			expectedVM:  true,
			expectedID:  "simple-vm",
			expectedName: "simple-vm",
		},
		{
			name: "kvm binary only",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/kvm",
				"-name",
				"guest=kvm-vm",
			},
			expectedVM:  true,
			expectedID:  "kvm-vm",
			expectedName: "kvm-vm",
		},
		{
			name: "Non-VM process (should not be detected)",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/firefox",
				"--profile",
				"/home/user/.mozilla/firefox",
			},
			expectedVM:  false,
			expectedID:  "",
			expectedName: "",
		},
	}

	allPassed := true

	for _, tc := range testCases {
		fmt.Printf("\n=== Testing: %s ===\n", tc.name)
		hypervisor, vmID := resource.VMInfoFromCmdLine(tc.cmdline)
		
		// Check if VM is detected
		isVM := hypervisor != resource.UnknownHypervisor
		
		fmt.Printf("Expected VM: %v | Detected VM: %v\n", tc.expectedVM, isVM)
		fmt.Printf("Hypervisor: %s\n", hypervisor)
		fmt.Printf("Expected ID: %s | Actual ID: %s\n", tc.expectedID, vmID)
		
		// Check VM name extraction
		vmName := qemuVMNameFromCmdLine(tc.cmdline)
		fmt.Printf("Expected Name: %s | Actual Name: %s\n", tc.expectedName, vmName)
		
		// Verify results
		if tc.expectedVM != isVM {
			fmt.Printf("❌ FAIL: VM detection mismatch\n")
			allPassed = false
		} else if tc.expectedVM && vmID != tc.expectedID {
			fmt.Printf("❌ FAIL: VM ID mismatch\n")
			allPassed = false
		} else if tc.expectedVM && vmName != tc.expectedName {
			fmt.Printf("❌ FAIL: VM Name mismatch\n")
			allPassed = false
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("✅ PASS\n")
		}
	}

	fmt.Printf("\n=== Summary ===\n")
	if allPassed {
		fmt.Printf("✅ All tests passed! The fix correctly handles CentOS/RHEL QEMU-KVM.\n")
		os.Exit(0)
	} else {
		fmt.Printf("❌ Some tests failed.\n")
		os.Exit(1)
	}
}

// Copy the qemuVMNameFromCmdLine function from vm.go for testing
func qemuVMNameFromCmdLine(cmdline []string) string {
	for i, arg := range cmdline {
		if arg == "-name" && i+1 < len(cmdline) {
			value := cmdline[i+1]
			// QEMU -name can have format "guest=name,debug-threads=on"
			if strings.Contains(value, "guest=") {
				parts := strings.Split(value, ",")
				for _, part := range parts {
					if strings.HasPrefix(part, "guest=") {
						return strings.TrimPrefix(part, "guest=")
					}
				}
			}
			return value
		}
		if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-name=") {
			return strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "-name=")
		}
	}
	return ""
}'

🎬 ACTION
str_replace_editor create /testbed/test_final_verification.go --file_text 'package main

import (
	"fmt"
	"path/filepath"
	"regexp"
	"strings"
)

func main() {
	// Test the new pattern
	qemuPattern := regexp.MustCompile(`(bin/qemu-system-\w+|qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm|qemu|kvm)`)
	
	testCases := []struct {
		name       string
		cmdline    []string
		shouldMatch bool
	}{
		{
			name: "CentOS/RHEL qemu-kvm (from PR description)",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
				"-name",
				"guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on",
			},
			shouldMatch: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Standard qemu-system-x86_64",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
				"-name",
				"guest=ubuntu-vm",
			},
			shouldMatch: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Alternative qemu-kvm path",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/qemu-kvm",
				"-name",
				"guest=test-vm",
			},
			shouldMatch: true,
		},
		{
			name: "Non-VM process",
			cmdline: []string{
				"/usr/bin/firefox",
				"--profile",
				"/home/user/.mozilla/firefox",
			},
			shouldMatch: false,
		},
	}

	allPassed := true
	
	fmt.Printf("Testing the new QEMU pattern: %s\n\n", qemuPattern.String())

	for _, tc := range testCases {
		fmt.Printf("Test: %s\n", tc.name)
		fmt.Printf("Command: %s\n", tc.cmdline[0])
		
		// Simulate vmInfoFromCmdLine logic
		exe := filepath.Base(tc.cmdline[0])
		fullCmd := strings.Join(tc.cmdline, " ")
		
		matchesExe := qemuPattern.MatchString(exe)
		matchesFullCmd := qemuPattern.MatchString(fullCmd)
		
		fmt.Printf("  Executable: %s (matches: %v)\n", exe, matchesExe)
		fmt.Printf("  Full command matches: %v\n", matchesFullCmd)
		
		detected := matchesExe || matchesFullCmd
		fmt.Printf("  VM detected: %v (expected: %v)\n", detected, tc.shouldMatch)
		
		if detected == tc.shouldMatch {
			fmt.Printf("  ✅ PASS\n\n")
		} else {
			fmt.Printf("  ❌ FAIL\n\n")
			allPassed = false
		}
	}

	if allPassed {
		fmt.Println("🎉 All tests passed! The fix successfully handles CentOS/RHEL QEMU-KVM.")
	} else {
		fmt.Println("❌ Some tests failed.")
	}
}'

+package main
+
+import (
+"fmt"
+"path/filepath"
+"strings"
+)
+
+func main() {
+// Test the exact command from the PR description
+centosCommand := []string{
+"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
+"-name",
+"guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on",
+"-S",
+"-object",
+`{"qom-type":"secret","id":"masterKey0","format":"raw","file":"/var/lib/libvirt/qemu/domain-25-instance-0000008b/master-key.aes"}`,
+"-machine",
+"pc-q35-rhel9.4.0,usb=off,dump-guest-core=off,hpet=off,acpi=on",
+"-accel",
+"kvm",
+"-cpu",
+"Broadwell-IBRS",
+}
+
+// Simulate what vmInfoFromCmdLine does
+exe := filepath.Base(centosCommand[0])
+fullCmd := strings.Join(centosCommand, " ")
+
+fmt.Printf("Executable: %s\n", exe)
+fmt.Printf("Executable matches qemu-kvm: %v\n", strings.Contains(exe, "qemu-kvm"))
+fmt.Printf("Full command contains 'qemu-kvm': %v\n", strings.Contains(fullCmd, "qemu-kvm"))
+fmt.Printf("Full command contains '-name guest=': %v\n", strings.Contains(fullCmd, "-name guest="))
+
+// Test with our new pattern
+qemuPattern := `(bin/qemu-system-\w+|qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm|qemu|kvm)`
+
+fmt.Printf("\nPattern would match executable: %v\n", matchPattern(exe, qemuPattern))
+fmt.Printf("Pattern would match full command: %v\n", matchPattern(fullCmd, qemuPattern))
+
+// Test VM name extraction
+fmt.Printf("\nWould extract VM name: %v\n", extractVMName(centosCommand))
+}
+
+func matchPattern(s, pattern string) bool {
+// Simplified pattern matching for testing
+patterns := []string{"qemu-system-", "qemu-kvm", "qemu", "kvm"}
+for _, p := range patterns {
+if strings.Contains(s, p) {
+return true
+}
+}
+return false
+}
+
+func extractVMName(cmdline []string) string {
+for i, arg := range cmdline {
+if arg == "-name" && i+1 < len(cmdline) {
+value := cmdline[i+1]
+if strings.Contains(value, "guest=") {
+parts := strings.Split(value, ",")
+for _, part := range parts {
+if strings.HasPrefix(part, "guest=") {
+return strings.TrimPrefix(part, "guest=")
+}
+}
+}
+return value
+}
+if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-name=") {
+return strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "-name=")
+}
+}
+return ""
+}

+package main
+
+import (
+"fmt"
+"os"
+"path/filepath"
+"strings"
+
+"github.com/sustainable-computing-io/kepler/internal/resource"
+)
+
+func main() {
+// Test cases based on the PR description and common CentOS/RHEL scenarios
+testCases := []struct {
+name        string
+cmdline     []string
+expectedVM  bool
+expectedID  string
+expectedName string
+}{
+{
+name: "CentOS/RHEL OpenStack QEMU-KVM (from PR description)",
+cmdline: []string{
+"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
+"-name", 
+"guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on",
+"-S",
+"-object",
+`{"qom-type":"secret","id":"masterKey0","format":"raw","file":"/var/lib/libvirt/qemu/domain-25-instance-0000008b/master-key.aes"}`,
+"-machine",
+"pc-q35-rhel9.4.0,usb=off,dump-guest-core=off,hpet=off,acpi=on",
+"-accel",
+"kvm",
+"-cpu",
+"Broadwell-IBRS",
+},
+expectedVM:  true,
+expectedID:  "instance-0000008b",
+expectedName: "instance-0000008b",
+},
+{
+name: "Standard QEMU system (original case)",
+cmdline: []string{
+"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
+"-name",
+"guest=ubuntu-vm",
+"-uuid",
+"12345678-1234-5678-9abc-123456789abc",
+},
+expectedVM:  true,
+expectedID:  "12345678-1234-5678-9abc-123456789abc",
+expectedName: "ubuntu-vm",
+},
+{
+name: "Alternative QEMU-KVM path",
+cmdline: []string{
+"/usr/bin/qemu-kvm",
+"-name",
+"guest=centos-vm",
+},
+expectedVM:  true,
+expectedID:  "centos-vm",
+expectedName: "centos-vm",
+},
+{
+name: "Simple qemu binary",
+cmdline: []string{
+"/usr/bin/qemu",
+"-name",
+"guest=simple-vm",
+},
+expectedVM:  true,
+expectedID:  "simple-vm",
+expectedName: "simple-vm",
+},
+{
+name: "kvm binary only",
+cmdline: []string{
+"/usr/bin/kvm",
+"-name",
+"guest=kvm-vm",
+},
+expectedVM:  true,
+expectedID:  "kvm-vm",
+expectedName: "kvm-vm",
+},
+{
+name: "Non-VM process (should not be detected)",
+cmdline: []string{
+"/usr/bin/firefox",
+"--profile",
+"/home/user/.mozilla/firefox",
+},
+expectedVM:  false,
+expectedID:  "",
+expectedName: "",
+},
+}
+
+allPassed := true
+
+for _, tc := range testCases {
+fmt.Printf("\n=== Testing: %s ===\n", tc.name)
+hypervisor, vmID := resource.VMInfoFromCmdLine(tc.cmdline)
+
+// Check if VM is detected
+isVM := hypervisor != resource.UnknownHypervisor
+
+fmt.Printf("Expected VM: %v | Detected VM: %v\n", tc.expectedVM, isVM)
+fmt.Printf("Hypervisor: %s\n", hypervisor)
+fmt.Printf("Expected ID: %s | Actual ID: %s\n", tc.expectedID, vmID)
+
+// Check VM name extraction
+vmName := qemuVMNameFromCmdLine(tc.cmdline)
+fmt.Printf("Expected Name: %s | Actual Name: %s\n", tc.expectedName, vmName)
+
+// Verify results
+if tc.expectedVM != isVM {
+fmt.Printf("❌ FAIL: VM detection mismatch\n")
+allPassed = false
+} else if tc.expectedVM && vmID != tc.expectedID {
+fmt.Printf("❌ FAIL: VM ID mismatch\n")
+allPassed = false
+} else if tc.expectedVM && vmName != tc.expectedName {
+fmt.Printf("❌ FAIL: VM Name mismatch\n")
+allPassed = false
+} else {
+fmt.Printf("✅ PASS\n")
+}
+}

+if allPassed {
+fmt.Printf("✅ All tests passed! The fix correctly handles CentOS/RHEL QEMU-KVM.\n")
+os.Exit(0)
+} else {
+fmt.Printf("❌ Some tests failed.\n")
+os.Exit(1)
+}

+// Copy the qemuVMNameFromCmdLine function from vm.go for testing
+func qemuVMNameFromCmdLine(cmdline []string) string {
+for i, arg := range cmdline {
+if arg == "-name" && i+1 < len(cmdline) {
+value := cmdline[i+1]
+// QEMU -name can have format "guest=name,debug-threads=on"
+if strings.Contains(value, "guest=") {
+parts := strings.Split(value, ",")
+for _, part := range parts {
+if strings.HasPrefix(part, "guest=") {
+return strings.TrimPrefix(part, "guest=")
+}
+}
+}
+return value
+}
+if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-name=") {
+return strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "-name=")
+}
+}
+return ""

+package main

+import (
+"fmt"
+"path/filepath"
+"regexp"
+"strings"
+)
+
+func main() {
+// Test the new pattern
+qemuPattern := regexp.MustCompile(`(bin/qemu-system-\w+|qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm|qemu|kvm)`)
+
+testCases := []struct {
+name       string
+cmdline    []string
+shouldMatch bool
+}{
+{
+name: "CentOS/RHEL qemu-kvm (from PR description)",
+cmdline: []string{
+"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",
+"-name",
+"guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on",
+},
+shouldMatch: true,
+},
+{
+name: "Standard qemu-system-x86_64",
+cmdline: []string{
+"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",
+"-name",
+"guest=ubuntu-vm",
+},
+shouldMatch: true,
+},
+{
+name: "Alternative qemu-kvm path",
+cmdline: []string{
+"/usr/bin/qemu-kvm",
+"-name",
+"guest=test-vm",
+},
+shouldMatch: true,
+},
+{
+name: "Non-VM process",
+cmdline: []string{
+"/usr/bin/firefox",
+"--profile",
+"/home/user/.mozilla/firefox",
+},
+shouldMatch: false,
+},
+}
+
+allPassed := true
+
+fmt.Printf("Testing the new QEMU pattern: %s\n\n", qemuPattern.String())
+
+for _, tc := range testCases {
+fmt.Printf("Test: %s\n", tc.name)
+fmt.Printf("Command: %s\n", tc.cmdline[0])
+
+// Simulate vmInfoFromCmdLine logic
+exe := filepath.Base(tc.cmdline[0])
+fullCmd := strings.Join(tc.cmdline, " ")
+
+matchesExe := qemuPattern.MatchString(exe)
+matchesFullCmd := qemuPattern.MatchString(fullCmd)
+
+fmt.Printf("  Executable: %s (matches: %v)\n", exe, matchesExe)
+fmt.Printf("  Full command matches: %v\n", matchesFullCmd)
+
+detected := matchesExe || matchesFullCmd
+fmt.Printf("  VM detected: %v (expected: %v)\n", detected, tc.shouldMatch)
+
+if detected == tc.shouldMatch {
+fmt.Printf("  ✅ PASS\n\n")
+} else {
+fmt.Printf("  ❌ FAIL\n\n")
+allPassed = false
+}
+}
+
+if allPassed {
+fmt.Println("🎉 All tests passed! The fix successfully handles CentOS/RHEL QEMU-KVM.")
+} else {
+fmt.Println("❌ Some tests failed.")
+}
+}

+package main
+
+import (
+"fmt"
+"regexp"
+)
+
+func main() {
+// Test cases representing different QEMU/KVM command lines
+testCases := []struct {
+name    string
+cmdline []string
+}{
+{
+name:    "Standard QEMU",
+cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64", "-name", "guest=vm1,debug-threads=on", "-machine", "pc"},
+},
+{
+name:    "CentOS/RHEL QEMU-KVM",
+cmdline: []string{"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm", "-name", "guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on", "-S", "-object"},
+},
+{
+name:    "Alternative QEMU-KVM",
+cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu-kvm", "-name", "guest=test-vm,debug-threads=on"},
+},
+{
+name:    "Simple QEMU",
+cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu", "-name", "guest=vm1"},
+},
+{
+name:    "KVM only",
+cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/kvm", "-name", "guest=vm1"},
+},
+}
+
+// Test different patterns
+patterns := []struct {
+name string
+regex string
+}{
+{"Current", `bin/qemu-system-\w+`},
+{"QEMU variants", `(qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm|qemu)`},
+{"Flexible QEMU/KVM", `(qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm|qemu|kvm)`},
+{"Flexible with paths", `(bin|libexec)/(qemu-system-\w+|qemu-kvm|qemu|kvm)`},
+}
+
+for _, pattern := range patterns {
+fmt.Printf("\n=== Testing pattern: %s (%s) ===\n", pattern.name, pattern.regex)
+re := regexp.MustCompile(pattern.regex)
+
+for _, tc := range testCases {
+exe := tc.cmdline[0]
+fullCmd := ""
+for _, arg := range tc.cmdline {
+fullCmd += arg + " "
+}
+
+matchesExe := re.MatchString(exe)
+matchesFull := re.MatchString(fullCmd)
+
+fmt.Printf("%-30s | exe: %-5v | full: %-5v | detected: %v\n", 
+tc.name, matchesExe, matchesFull, matchesExe || matchesFull)
+}
+}
+}

+package main
+
+import (
+"fmt"
+"regexp"
+)
+
+func main() {
+// Current pattern from vm.go
+qemuPattern := regexp.MustCompile(`bin/qemu-system-\w+`)
+
+// Test cases
+testCases := []string{
+"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",  // Standard Linux path
+"/bin/qemu-system-x86_64",      // Alternative path
+"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm",        // CentOS/RHEL path (this should match but doesn't)
+"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm-core",   // Possible variation
+"/usr/bin/qemu-kvm",            // Another possible path
+"/bin/kvm",                     // Simple kvm binary
+}
+
+fmt.Println("Testing current pattern:")
+for _, test := range testCases {
+matches := qemuPattern.MatchString(test)
+fmt.Printf("%-30s matches: %v\n", test, matches)
+}
+
+// Test with full command lines
+fmt.Println("\nTesting with full command lines:")
+fullCommands := []string{
+"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm -name guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on -S -object",
+"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64 -name guest=vm1,debug-threads=on",
+}
+
+for _, cmd := range fullCommands {
+matches := qemuPattern.MatchString(cmd)
+fmt.Printf("%-60s matches: %v\n", cmd, matches)
+}
+}

+package main
+
+import (
+"fmt"
+"regexp"
+)
+
+func main() {
+// Test cases representing different QEMU/KVM command lines
+testCases := []struct {
+name    string
+cmdline []string
+}{
+{
+name:    "Standard QEMU",
+cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu-system-x86_64", "-name", "guest=vm1,debug-threads=on", "-machine", "pc"},
+},
+{
+name:    "CentOS/RHEL QEMU-KVM",
+cmdline: []string{"/usr/libexec/qemu-kvm", "-name", "guest=instance-0000008b,debug-threads=on", "-S", "-object"},
+},
+{
+name:    "Alternative QEMU-KVM",
+cmdline: []string{"/usr/bin/qemu-kvm", "-name", "guest=test-vm,debug-threads=on"},
+},
+}
+
+for _, tc := range testCases {
+fmt.Printf("\nTest: %s\n", tc.name)
+fmt.Printf("Command line: %v\n", tc.cmdline)
+
+// This simulates what vmInfoFromCmdLine does
+extractedInfo(tc.cmdline)
+}
+}
+
+func extractedInfo(cmdline []string) {
+// Simulate the vmInfoFromCmdLine logic
+exe := cmdline[0]
+fullCmd := ""
+for _, arg := range cmdline {
+fullCmd += arg + " "
+}
+
+// Use actual regex patterns like in vm.go
+qemuPattern := regexp.MustCompile(`bin/qemu-system-\w+`)
+
+matchesExe := qemuPattern.MatchString(exe)
+matchesFull := qemuPattern.MatchString(fullCmd)
+
+fmt.Printf("Executable: %s\n", exe)
+fmt.Printf("Matches executable: %v\n", matchesExe)
+fmt.Printf("Matches full command: %v\n", matchesFull)
+fmt.Printf("Detected as VM: %v\n", matchesExe || matchesFull)
+}

+                        value := cmdline[i+1]
+                        // QEMU -name can have format "guest=name,debug-threads=on"
+                        if strings.Contains(value, "guest=") {
+                                parts := strings.Split(value, ",")
+
+                                for _, part := range parts {
+                                        if strings.HasPrefix(part, "guest=") {
+                                                return strings.TrimPrefix(part, "guest=")
+                                        }
+                                }
+                        }
+                        return value
+                }
+
+                if strings.HasPrefix(arg, "-name=") {
+                        return strings.TrimPrefix(arg, "-name=")
+                }
+        }
+        return ""
 }
